 vah bahumukhi pratibha ke dhani or pragatisheel vichaardhaara vaale vyakti the
 Charan Singh was born on 23 December 1902 in a Jat family in Noorpur village of Ghaziabad district
 unhone swadhinata andolan ke samay raajnneeti main pravesh kiya

 Impressed by the 'full Swarajya' proclamation of the Lahore session of the Congress in 1929, young Charan Singh formed the Congress Committee in Ghaziabad
 san 1930 main mahatma gandhi ke chalaae savinay avagya andolan main shaamil hokar unhone namak kanoon todane ko dandi march kiya
 Charan Singh, the madman of independence, made salt on the Hindon river flowing on the border of Ghaziabad
 is kaaran charan singh ko 6 maah kaid kii sajaa hui

 san 1940 ke vyaktigat satyagrah main bhi charan singh giraftaar hue

 9 agast, 1942 ko agast kranti ke maahaul main yuva charan singh ne bhumigat hokar gupt krantikari sanghathan taiyaar kiya
 In Meerut Commissionerate, Charan Singh, along with revolutionary colleagues, repeatedly challenged the British rule
 meerut prashasan ne charan singh ko dekhte hi goli maarane kaa aadesh de rakhaa tha

 aakhirkaar police ne ek din charan singh ko giraftaar kar hi liya
 Sentenced to one and a half years as Rajbandi
 jail main hi choudhary charan singh kii likhit pustak shishtachar, bhartiya samskruti or samaaj ke shishtachar ke niyamon kaa ek bahumoolya dastavej he
 Chaudhary Charan Singh has been considered the leader of farmers
 unke dwaara taiyaar kiya gaya jameendaari unmoolan vidheyak rajya ke kalyankari siddhant par aadhaarit tha
 On 1 July 1952, due to his abolition of Zamindari system in Uttar Pradesh, the poor got rights
 kisaanon ke hit main unhone 1954 main uttar pradesh bhoomi sangrakshan kanoon ko paarit karaayaa
 His image in the Congress was established as a skilled leader
 desh kii aazaadee ke baad vah rashtriya str ke netaa to nahin ban sake, lekin rajya vidhansabha main unka prabhaav spasht mahasoos kiya jaataa tha

 san 1952 main dow
 During Sampurnanand's Chief Ministership, he got the responsibility of Revenue and Agriculture Department
 vah jameen se jude netaa the or krishi vibhaag unhen vishisht rup se pasand tha
 Charan Singh was also a farmer by nature
 vah krishak hiton ke liye anwarat prayaas karte rahe
 In 1960, he was given the Ministry of Home and Agriculture under Chandrabhanu Gupta's government

 The farmers of Uttar Pradesh began to consider Charan Singh as their messiah
 unhone krishakon ke kalyaan ke liye kaaphi kaary kiye

 uttar pradesh ke gramin ilaakon main krishi mukhya vyavsaay tha
 Due to respect among farmers, they did not face defeat in any election
 charan singh kii eemaandaarana koshishon kii sadaiv saraahna hui
 He was more of a social worker than a politician for the people
 unhen bhaashankala main bhi maharath hasil thi

 choudhary sahab 3 april, 1967 main pehali baar uttar pradesh ke mukhyamantri bane the
 At that time, due to the threat of his decisive administrative ability and the public was confident that despite the riots in 1967, there was no leaf in Uttar Pradesh
 17 april, 1968 ko unhone mukhyamantri ke pad se istipha de diya

 unhone apane siddhanton va maryaadit aacharan se kabhi samjhauta nahin kiya

 centre sarkaar main grahamantri bane to unhone mandal va alpsankhyak ayog kii sthapana kii

 baad main morarji desai or charan singh ke bich matbhed ho gaya

 unka angreji bhashaa par acha adhikaar tha

 The Left parties said that it is unfortunate that the Election Commission and its mechanism remained a mute spectator of democracy and rape in West Bengal
 varisht netaaon seetaram yechuri or es ramchandran pillai kii ore se chunaav ayog ke sheersh adhikariyon ko saunpe gaye gyaapan main kaha gaya ki swatantra or nishpaksh chunaav karaane ke sanvaidhanik adhikaar ke nirvahan se pare ayog laachaar tamaashai bana rahaa
 Yechury said that the Left parties will stage a protest in the state tomorrow and will also agitate in other parts of the country
 unhone bataaya ki jin 800 boothon par punarmatdaan kii maang kii gai he ve 17 loksabhaa siton main se prayek seat kaa lagbhag 7 pratishat vot he jo bahut mahatvapurn he
 Voting on these seats took place today
